---
title: "Gnome Unresponsive (ATI 4850)"
date: 2009-10-02
forum: General Help
---

### Post by richiejenkins on 2009-10-02
Hey,

I installed Ubuntu 9.04 64 bit today, but I have found gnome very unresponsive. I believe it might be the something to do with my ATI HD4850 as everything else seems to be fine.

Sometimes when clicking on opening a window from the system bar it won't do the animation effects and takes around 2 seconds to load.

Have installed ATI Drivers from ATI Website and also have 3D Enabled.

Any help would be great. 

Thanks

System:
Intel Core 2 Quad Q8400 2.6Ghz
2 X 2GB @ 1066Mhz
ATI HD4850
250GB 16MB Cache 7200RPM
500W PSU

**UPDATE:**

Just done a fresh install of Ubuntu 9.04, problem still there. When going opening the display manger it sort of crashes and takes forever to load (around 40 seconds).

### Post by bwang on 2009-10-02
Have you tried using EnvyNG to install the drivers?
Also, could you post the contents of your Xorg log?
```
cat /var/log/Xorg.0.log
```
